 1

 2

 3
 Mention about the old job only when you are asked about it

 If you have any questions related to the company, ask it very easily

 Before answering the question, start talking with Sir / Madam for the address

 While talking on the phone, keep your words clearly in short words

 When does worship of Pujagangaur begin on the second day of Holi (chaitra Krishna Pratipada)
 is din se mahilaayein pratidin gangaur ko puujati hai or caitra shukla dwitiya (sinjaare) ke din nadi, talab yaa sarovar par jaakar puji hui ganagauron ko pani pilaati hai
